management through a coordinated system across the group-coordinator and core modules. The architecture consists of four main components:\\n\\n1. **OffsetAndMetadata Storage**: The `OffsetAndMetadata` class (group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/OffsetAndMetadata.java) represents a committed offset with its metadata, including the offset value, leader epoch, custom metadata string, commit timestamp, and expiration timestamp. These offsets are stored in the __consumer_offsets topic as records with `OffsetCommitKey` and `OffsetCommitValue` schema types.\\n\\n2. **GroupCoordinator Offset Commit Handler**: The `OffsetMetadataManager` (group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/OffsetMetadataManager.java) manages offset commits and fetches. When offset commit requests arrive via `handleOffsetCommitRequest` in KafkaApis (core/src/main/scala/kafka/server/KafkaApis.scala), they are routed to the GroupCoordinator, which delegates to OffsetMetadataManager. The manager generates `OffsetCommitValue` records using `GroupCoordinatorRecordHelpers.newOffsetCommitRecord` (group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/GroupCoordinatorRecordHelpers.java), which are then appended to the __consumer_offsets partition via `CoordinatorPartitionWriter` (core/src/main/scala/kafka/coordinator/group/CoordinatorPartitionWriter.scala).\\n\\n3. **OffsetFetch Request Processor**: The `handleOffsetFetchRequest` in KafkaApis processes OffsetFetch requests and retrieves committed offsets through the GroupCoordinator's offset fetching logic in `OffsetMetadataManager`. This supports both modern consumer groups and legacy classic groups, returning the committed offset and metadata for each partition.\\n\\n4. **Offset Expiry and Compaction Logic**: The `OffsetExpirationCondition` and `OffsetExpirationConditionImpl` classes (group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/OffsetExpirationCondition.java and OffsetExpirationConditionImpl.java) define when offsets expire based on retention time. The `OffsetMetadataManager` includes methods to remove expired offsets and generates tombstone records via `newOffsetCommitTombstoneRecord` to compact the __consumer_offsets log. The `GroupCoordinatorConfig` (group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/GroupCoordinatorConfig.java) manages retention configuration.\\n\\n5. **Offset Loading and Replay**: During broker startup or coordinator failover, the `CoordinatorLoaderImpl` (core/src/main/scala/kafka/coordinator/group/CoordinatorLoaderImpl.scala) reads offset records from the __consumer_offsets log and replays them through the `OffsetMetadataManager.replay` method to reconstruct the in-memory offset state.
